\index{check\_hash@{check\_hash}!cryptonote@{cryptonote}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{check\_hash()}{check\_hash()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{stdbool_8h_a1062901a7428fdd9c7f180f5e01ea056}{bool}} cryptonote\+::check\+\_\+hash (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structcrypto_1_1hash}{crypto\+::hash}} \&}]{hash,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacecryptonote_afa000315dc9cabb236f0b077dc812d6e}{difficulty\+\_\+type}}}]{difficulty }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



checks if a hash fits the given difficulty 

The hash passes if (hash $\ast$ difficulty) $<$ 2$^\wedge$256. Phrased differently, if (hash $\ast$ difficulty) fits without overflow into the least significant 256 bits of the 320 bit multiplication result.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em hash} & the hash to check \\
\hline
{\em difficulty} & the difficulty to check against\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if valid, else false 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacecryptonote_abe0df1b7866c9e552d02596033ea1701}\label{namespacecryptonote_abe0df1b7866c9e552d02596033ea1701}} 
\index{cryptonote@{cryptonote}!generate\_multisig\_derivations@{generate\_multisig\_derivations}}
\index{generate\_multisig\_derivations@{generate\_multisig\_derivations}!cryptonote@{cryptonote}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{generate\_multisig\_derivations()}{generate\_multisig\_derivations()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcrypto_1_1public__key}{crypto\+::public\+\_\+key}} $>$ cryptonote\+::generate\+\_\+multisig\+\_\+derivations (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structcryptonote_1_1account__keys}{account\+\_\+keys}} \&}]{keys,  }\item[{const std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcrypto_1_1public__key}{crypto\+::public\+\_\+key}} $>$ \&}]{derivations }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



generate\+\_\+multisig\+\_\+derivations performs common DH key derivation. Each middle round in M/N scheme is DH exchange of public multisig keys of other participants multiplied by secret spend key of current participant. this functions does the following\+: new multisig key = secret spend $\ast$ public multisig key 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em keys} & -\/ current wallet\textquotesingle{}s keys \\
\hline
{\em derivations} & -\/ public multisig keys of other participants \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
new public multisig keys derived from previous round. This data needs to be exchange with other participants 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacecryptonote_a68169276fdf2584c819ead8e2134c339}\label{namespacecryptonote_a68169276fdf2584c819ead8e2134c339}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{init\_key()}{init\_key()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Privkey , typename Pubkey , typename Get\+Pubkey , typename Generate\+Pair $>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{stdbool_8h_a1062901a7428fdd9c7f180f5e01ea056}{bool}} cryptonote\+::init\+\_\+key (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const fs\+::path \&}]{keypath,  }\item[{Privkey \&}]{privkey,  }\item[{Pubkey \&}]{pubkey,  }\item[{Get\+Pubkey}]{get\+\_\+pubkey,  }\item[{Generate\+Pair}]{generate\+\_\+pair }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Loads a key pair from disk, if it exists, otherwise generates a new key pair and saves it to disk.

get\+\_\+pubkey -\/ a function taking (privkey \&, pubkey \&) that sets the pubkey from the privkey; returns true for success/false for failure generate\+\_\+pair -\/ a void function taking (privkey \&, pubkey \&) that sets them to the generated values; can throw on error. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacecryptonote_a86b85cd11f902061c036b6cad55093f4}\label{namespacecryptonote_a86b85cd11f902061c036b6cad55093f4}}
